BZHIN GSHEGS PA BLO GROS DAM PAR DGONGS PA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE
BZHIN GSHEGS PA YON TAN GYIS

PO LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA YE SHES BLO GROS LA
PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA

YON TAN RI RAB LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA DBYANGS
SNYAN PA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA G-YUL 'JIGS PA LA
PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS

PA GSAL BA'I DPAL LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA ZLA BA
STON PA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA YON TAN PHUNG PO
RAB TU SNANG BA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE

BZHIN GSHEGS PA CHOS KYI STOBS LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN
GSHEGS PA THE TSOM RNAM PAR ZHI BA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN
GSHEGS PA RNAM PAR GRAGS PA'I RGYAL PO

LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA DBANG PO DUL BA LA PHYAG
'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA BLO GROS MCHOG LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO,
,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA BDUD RTZI'I DBANG


@234B PA LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA BDUD RTZI'I 'OD
LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA BDUD RTZIR DGONGS PA LA
PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA YON TAN 'OD KYI RGYAL PO

PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA PHUN SUM GRAGS PA LA PHYAG
'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA KUN TU GSAL

PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA BRTZON 'GRUS MTHA' YAS PA LA

@235A *, ,KYIS DE'I TSE TSOGS SU BCAD PA 'DI GSUNGS SO, ,RGYAL BA
RNAMS KYI MTSAN 'DI THOS NA NI, ,BAG YOD RIM GRO BSKYED CING RIG
PAR BYA, ,PHUN SUM 'DI LA MA DAD

SPONG NA NI, ,NGAN SONG SDUG BSNGAL PHYIR YANG MYONG NGA RE, ,RIM
BZHIN TSUL KHRIMS LA NI BRTEN NAS SU, ,THOS LA DAD CING RAB TU
DBEN PAR LDAN, ,ZAB MO BZOD PA YONGS SU BKANG NAS NI, ,

DES NI 'JIG RTEN MGON PO 'DI KUN MTHONG, ,LAS KYI 'BRAS BU RNAM
SMIN MI SHES TE, ,BSKAL PA BYE BAR SDIG PA'I LAS BYAS PAS, ,RGYAL
BA RNAMS LA MOS PAS MTSAN BRJOD NA, ,DE

DAG KUN GYI SRAS SU DE 'GYUR RO, ,SANGS RGYAS KYI MTSAN LNGA
